(function(_cc_end_point) {
  var transactionId;
  try {
    // returns null if _tidSto not in session storage
    transactionId = window.sessionStorage.getItem('_tidSto');
  } catch(err) {}

  // No session detected, generate a fresh tid and cc.js
  if (!transactionId) {

    // Generate a new session id
    var d = new Date().getTime();
    var _tid = 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function(c) {
      var r = (d + Math.random() * 16) % 16 | 0;
      d = Math.floor(d / 16);
      return (c == 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8)).toString(16);
    });
    _tid = "HOME_" + _tid;

    // _tid global for reference in login-badge-service and _ease-signin.service
    window._tid = _tid;

    // Add _tid to session storage
    try {
      window.sessionStorage.setItem('_tidSto', _tid);
    } catch(err) {}

    var _siteKey = "b57e9686e0bc24f0";
    var _cc = _cc || [];
    _cc.push(['ci', {
      'sid': _siteKey,
      'tid': _tid
    }]);
    _cc.push(['cf', 334835]);
    _cc.push(['run', _cc_end_point]);

    // Attach _cc to window for cc.js script to reference
    window._cc = _cc;

    // Append device profile script
    var c = document.createElement('script');
    c.type = 'text/javascript';
    c.async = true;
    c.src = _cc_end_point + '/cc.js?tid=' + _tid;
    var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
    s.parentNode.insertBefore(c, s);

  } else {
    // Sessions exists, re-attach _tid to window
    window._tid = transactionId;
  }

})('https://deviceinfo.capitalone.com/collector');

</script>

    var segments = {
            venture: {
                exp: 5,
                hero: 5,
                zoneB: 5,
                zoneC: 5,
                zoneD: 5
            },
            northstarA: {
                exp: 5,
                hero: 11,
                zoneB: 11,
                zoneC: 11,
                zoneD: 5
            },
            northstarB: {
                exp: 5,
                hero: 11,
                zoneB: 12,
                zoneC: 11,
                zoneD: 5
            },
            northstarC: {
                exp: 5,
                hero: 5,
                zoneB: 13,
                zoneC: 5,
                zoneD: 5
            },
            cardCompare: {
                exp: 5,
                hero: 12,
                zoneB: 5,
                zoneC: 5,
                zoneD: 5
            }

    }

    function setExperience(exp) {
        if (!exp.hero) { exp.hero = exp.exp };
        if (!exp.zoneB) { exp.zoneB = exp.exp };
        if (!exp.zoneC) { exp.zoneC = exp.exp };
        if (!exp.zoneD) { exp.zoneD = exp.exp };
        document.querySelector("body").setAttribute("EXP", exp.exp);
        document.querySelector("body").setAttribute("HERO", exp.hero);
        document.querySelector("body").setAttribute("ZONEB", exp.zoneB);
        document.querySelector("body").setAttribute("ZONEC", exp.zoneC);
        document.querySelector("body").setAttribute("ZONED", exp.zoneD);
        window.siteCatVar = exp.sitecat ? exp.sitecat : null;
    }

    function setHeroSegment(){
        var prospect_exps = [],
        total_weight = 100,
        current_weight = 0,
        random_num = Math.floor(Math.random() * (100 - 1) + 1);
        prospect_exps[5] = 33.33;
        prospect_exps[8] = 33.33;
        prospect_exps[9] = 33.33;
        var heros = [5, 8, 9];
        for (var i in heros) {
            current_weight += prospect_exps[heros[i]];
            if (current_weight > random_num) {
                experience = heros[i];
                return experience;
            }
        }
    }

    function setHeroExperience(hero){
        if(!hero){
            hero = setHeroSegment();
        }
        setExperience({exp:5, hero:hero});
    }

    setHeroExperience();

</script>

<script>
   (function smartBanner () {
     /*
     ** iOS Devices
     ** Utilizes a meta tag to render a safari smart banner, not accessible
     ** within the dom (iOS magic). BC this does not require the template ele,
     ** and only the meta tag, create tag, and destroy the template.
     */

     var smartLink = 'https://smart.link/';
     var kochavaSmartLinkMap = {
         '/': {
             smartLinkId: "58769937fc597"
         },
         '/ent-signin/': {
             smartLinkId: "589a10bc405f4"
         },
         '/ent-spanish/': {
             smartLinkId: "589a4207855a0"
         }
     }

     function addKochavaSmartlink () {
         var path = window.location.pathname;
         var smartLinkId = kochavaSmartLinkMap[path].smartLinkId;
         $('body').append('<img src="' + smartLink + smartLinkId + '" height="1" width="1" border ="0" />');
     }

     if (window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.os !== undefined && window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.os.indexOf('iPhone') !== -1) {
         // Create the iOS meta tag.
         var iosMeta = document.createElement('meta');
         iosMeta.name = "apple-itunes-app";
         iosMeta.content = "app-id=407558537";
         document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(iosMeta);
         // Kochava tracking
         addKochavaSmartlink();
         // Destroy the element. (Not needed for iOS)
         $('#smartbanner').remove();
     }

     else if (window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.os !== undefined && window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.os.indexOf('Android') !== -1) {
         // Check localStorage, if item is expired, proceed to setup watcher.
         $('#smartbanner').css('display', 'block');
         checkLocalStorage();
         closeBannerWatcher();
         $('.sb-close').removeAttr('target');
         // Kochava tracking
         addKochavaSmartlink();
     }

     /*
     ** Unsupported Devices
     ** It's not android/iOS, destroy the element.
     */

     else {
       $('#smartbanner').remove();
     }

     /*
     ** Helpers
     */

     // Checks local storage to proceed based on item expiration.
     function checkLocalStorage() {
       var sbLocal = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('sbClose'));
       if (sbLocal) {
         if (sbLocal.closed && sbLocal.expiration > Date.now()) {
           $('#smartbanner').remove();
           return false;
         } else if (sbLocal.closed && sbLocal.expiration < Date.now()) {
           localStorage.removeItem('sbClose');
         }
       }
     }

     // Initialize a watcher for closing the smart banner.
     function closeBannerWatcher() {
         $('.sb-close').on('click', function() {
           // Destroy the element.
           $('#smartbanner').remove();

           // Set ExpirationDate = current time + 14 days.
           var expirationDate = Date.now();
           expirationDate += 1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 14;

           // Create object, and set in localStorage.
           var localStorageItem = {
             closed: true,
             expiration: expirationDate
           }
           localStorage.setItem('sbClose', JSON.stringify(localStorageItem));
         });
     }
   })();
</script>

    "nativeApp": "/applications/mobile/",

    "creditWiseApp": "https://control.kochava.com/v1/cpi/click?campaign_id=kocredit-tracker-android-prod560460d0adb3c93874dcc957c2&network_id=3536&device_id=device_id&site_id=1&append_app_conv_trk_params=1"
  },
  "defaults": {
    "nativeApp": "/applications/mobile/",
    "walletApp": "/applications/mobile/wallet/",
    "creditWiseApp": "/credit-cards/benefits/creditwise/"
  }
};
/*
** Mobile Devices
** Checks for c1SiteVars to determine if on a mobile device, will show
** the mobile taskbar accordingly.
*/
$(".mobile-utility-nav > li:not(.signin) > a").click(function(e) {e.preventDefault()});
$(document).ready(function(){

  if (window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.type !== undefined && window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.type.indexOf('mobile') !== -1) {
    $('#mobile-navigation').css('display', 'block');
    mobileTaskbarPortedScripts();
    // Changes the links to the app based on OS. If not ios or android links
    // landing page of the app.
    if (window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.os !== undefined && window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.os.indexOf('iPhone') !== -1) {
      $('.homepage-app-links-nativeApp').attr('href', mobileTaskbarApps.ios.nativeApp);
      $('.homepage-app-links-walletApp').attr('href', mobileTaskbarApps.ios.walletApp);
      $('.homepage-app-links-creditWiseApp').attr('href', mobileTaskbarApps.ios.creditWiseApp);

    } else if (window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.os !== undefined && window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.os.indexOf('Android') !== -1) {
      $('.homepage-app-links-nativeApp').attr('href', mobileTaskbarApps.android.nativeApp);
      $('.homepage-app-links-walletApp').attr('href', mobileTaskbarApps.android.walletApp);
      $('.homepage-app-links-creditWiseApp').attr('href', mobileTaskbarApps.android.creditWiseApp);
    } else {
      $('.homepage-app-links-nativeApp').attr('href', mobileTaskbarApps.defaults.nativeApp);
      $('.homepage-app-links-walletApp').attr('href', mobileTaskbarApps.defaults.walletApp);
      $('.homepage-app-links-creditWiseApp').attr('href', mobileTaskbarApps.defaults.creditWiseApp);
    }
  }
  /*
  ** Unsupported Devices
  ** Not mobile, destroy the element.
  */
  else {
    $('#mobile-navigation').remove();
  }
  /*
  ** Helper
  */
  function mobileTaskbarPortedScripts () {
    var t = $(".mobile-utility-nav").offset().top,
        i = $(window).height() - t;

    $(window).bind("scroll", function() {
      $(window).scrollTop() > t ? $(".mobile-utility-nav").addClass("fixed") : $(".mobile-utility-nav").removeClass("fixed")
    }),
    $(".mobile-utility-nav > li:not(.signin) > a").click(function(t) {
      t.preventDefault(),
      $(this).parent("li").hasClass("active") ?
        ($(this).parent("li").removeClass("active"), $(this).next(".content").removeAttr("style")) :
        ($(this).parent().parent().find("li").removeClass("active"), $(this).parent("li").addClass("active"), $(this).next(".content").css("height", i)), $("li.hasChildren").siblings().removeClass("on").children("ul").slideUp()
    }),
    $(".utility-menu li.hasChildren > a").click(function(t) {
      t.preventDefault(),
      $(this).parent().siblings().removeClass("on").children("ul").slideUp(),
      $(this).parent().hasClass("on") ? ($(this).parent().removeClass("on"),
      $(this).parent().children("ul").slideUp()) : ($(this).parent().addClass("on"),
      $(this).parent().children("ul").slideDown())
    }),
    $(".content > .utility-nav-callout > span.menu-close > a").click(function(t) {
      t.preventDefault(), $(this).closest("li").removeClass("active")
    });
  }
});

</script>

        if(c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.type !== 'mobile') {
          var pageMeta = JSON.parse($('[andromeda-page-meta]').attr('andromeda-page-meta'));

          if(pageMeta.block_headerFooter_header) {
            var headerObjFields = pageMeta.block_headerFooter_header.fields,
                $body = $('body'),
                $searchObj = $('#search-toggle'),
                $primaryNav = $('#navWrapper'),
                $lobObj = $('#' + headerObjFields.lob);
            $body.attr('show-header', headerObjFields.header);

            $searchObj ? $searchObj.attr('show-search', headerObjFields.search):false;
            $primaryNav ? $primaryNav.attr('primary-nav', headerObjFields.primaryNavigation):false;

            if ($body.attr('show-header') !== 'no-header' ) {
              $lobObj ? $lobObj.css('display', 'block'): $('.nav-audience')[0].css('display', 'block');
            }
          }
          else {
            $('body').attr('show-header', 'no-header');
          }
        }
    } catch(e) {
        console.error('NAVIGATION PRE-LOAD ERROR:', e);

    <script type="text/javascript">
  // load images after exp set
  // contact pages dont use templates (have html in contentful) so no lazy loading.
  // custom lazy image loader
  loadImages();

  function loadImages(){
    if(window.jQuery){
      var domExp =  'EXP:' + document.querySelector("body").getAttribute("EXP");
      var domHero = 'HERO:' + document.querySelector("body").getAttribute("HERO");
      var domZoneB = 'ZONEB:' + document.querySelector("body").getAttribute("ZONEB");
      var domZoneC = 'ZONEC:' + document.querySelector("body").getAttribute("ZONEC");
      var domZoneD = 'ZONED:' + document.querySelector("body").getAttribute("ZONED");
      // var domCtas = 'CTAS:' + document.querySelector("body").getAttribute("CTAS");

      $("[lazy-load-src]").each(function(){
        var parentDiv = $(this).parents("div[segment]")[0];
        var parentAttr = parentDiv.getAttribute("segment");
        if((parentAttr === domExp) || (parentAttr === domHero)|| (parentAttr === domZoneB) || (parentAttr === domZoneC) || (parentAttr === domZoneD)){
          var lazyLoadSrcUrl = $(this).attr("lazy-load-src");
          // if device type tablet and tablet image provided, load tablet image
          if (window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.type.indexOf('tablet') !== -1) {
              if ($(this).attr("tablet-load-src") !== undefined) {
                  lazyLoadSrcUrl = $(this).attr("tablet-load-src") + "?q=80";
              }
          }
          // if device type mobile and mobile image provided, load mobile image
          else if (window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.type.indexOf('mobile') !== -1) {
              // display tablet assets for mobile landscape orientation
              var query = window.matchMedia("(orientation:landscape)");
              if (query.matches) {
                  if ($(this).attr("tablet-load-src") !== undefined) {
                      lazyLoadSrcUrl = $(this).attr("tablet-load-src") + "?q=80";
                  }
              } else {
                  if ($(this).attr("mobile-load-src") !== undefined) {
                      lazyLoadSrcUrl = $(this).attr("mobile-load-src") + "?q=80";
                  }
              }
          }
          // if img set src, if div set bg image
          if($(this).is("img")){
            $(this).attr("src",lazyLoadSrcUrl);
          } else if($(this).is("div")){
            setCorrectlySizedBGImage(this, lazyLoadSrcUrl);
          } else if($(this).is("source")){
            $(this).attr("srcset",lazyLoadSrcUrl);
          }
        }
      });
    } else {
      // Safety net, only happens on slow browsers like ie11,if spectrum fails code executes before jquery.
      setTimeout(function() { loadImages() }, 50);
    }
  }

  // Reload images on orientation change for mobile device types
  if (document.addEventListener && window.c1SiteVars.deviceInfo.type.indexOf('mobile') !== -1) {
    window.addEventListener("orientationchange", function() {
      loadImages();
    }, false);
  }

  function setCorrectlySizedBGImage(node, url) {

    // Prevent duplicate query params
    if(url.indexOf("?q=80") !== -1 || url.indexOf("q=100") !== -1) {
      return $(node).css("background-image", "url("+url+")");
    } else {
      if(window.matchMedia("(min-width:48em)").matches) {
        return $(node).css("background-image", "url("+url+"&q=100)");
      } else {
        return $(node).css("background-image", "url("+url+"&q=80)");
      }
    }

  }
</script>
